This codebase represents the modern implementation using `path()` and `re_path()` functions.\\n\\n### Core URL Configuration Files\\n\\n**django/urls/__init__.py** - Main module that exports all public URL routing APIs including `path`, `re_path`, `include`, `URLPattern`, `URLResolver`, `ResolverMatch`, `LocalePrefixPattern`, and utility functions like `get_resolver()`, `get_ns_resolver()`, `resolve()`, and `reverse()`.\\n\\n**django/urls/conf.py** - Functions for URL configuration:\\n  - `include(arg, namespace=None)` (line 17): Takes a URLconf module, list, or tuple and returns a 3-tuple `(urlconf_module, app_name, namespace)`. `pattern`: A pattern object (RegexPattern or RoutePattern)\\n  - `callback`: The view function\\n  - `default_args`: Default keyword arguments\\n  - `name`: Optional name for URL reversal\\n  - `resolve()` method: Matches incoming paths and returns ResolverMatch\\n\\n**URLResolver** (line 503): Represents a hierarchy of URL patterns with:\\n  - `resolve()` method: Recursively resolves paths by iterating through url_patterns\\n  - `_populate()` method: Builds reverse lookup dictionaries for efficient URL reversal\\n  - `url_patterns` property: Loads patterns from urlconf_module.urlpatterns or returns the module itself\\n\\n**RegexPattern** (line 192): Pattern matching using compiled regular expressions\\n  - Uses `LocaleRegexDescriptor` for lazy compilation\\n  - `match()` method: Uses regex.search() for non-endpoint patterns or regex.fullmatch() for endpoints\\n  - Returns remaining path, positional args, and kwargs from named groups\\n\\n**RoutePattern** (line 314): Pattern matching using simplified path syntax (e.g., `<int:pk>`)\\n  - Uses `_route_to_regex()` to convert path syntax to regex\\n  - Manages converters that transform captured values (IntConverter, SlugConverter, etc.)\\n  - `match()` method: Converts values using registered converters\\n\\n**LocalePrefixPattern** (line 388): Special pattern for i18n language prefixes\\n  - `view_name`: Fully qualified view name\\n\\n### URL Dispatcher (django/urls/base.py)\\n\\n**resolve(path, urlconf=None)** (line 22): Entry point for URL resolution\\n  - Gets the root URLResolver via `get_resolver()`\\n  - Calls `resolver.resolve(path)` to match against urlpatterns\\n  - Returns ResolverMatch with matched view and arguments\\n\\n**reverse(viewname, ...)** (line 28): Reverse URL lookup\\n  - Resolves view names including namespaces (e.g., 'app:view')\\n  - Uses cached `_reverse_dict` in URLResolver for efficient lookup\\n  - Handles namespace resolution through `_namespace_dict`\\n  - Supports app-specific namespace resolution through `_app_dict`\\n\\n**get_resolver(urlconf=None)** (django/urls/resolvers.py, line 108): Returns cached URLResolver\\n  - Used for capturing parameters in namespace patterns\\n  - Wraps a resolver with namespace-specific pattern information\\n\\n### Supporting Components\\n\\n**django/urls/converters.py**: Path parameter converters\\n  - IntConverter: Matches `[0-9]+`\\n  - StringConverter: Matches `[^/]+`\\n  - SlugConverter: Matches `[-a-zA-Z0-9_]+`\\n  - PathConverter: Matches `.+`\\n  - UUIDConverter: Matches UUID format\\n  - `register_converter()`: Allows custom converters\\n\\n**django/urls/utils.py**: Utility functions\\n  - `get_callable(lookup_view)`: Converts string view paths to callables\\n  - `get_mod_func(callback)`: Splits 'module.function' strings\\n\\n**django/urls/exceptions.py**: Exception classes\\n  - `Resolver404`: Raised when URL doesn't match any pattern\\n  - `NoReverseMatch`: Raised when reverse lookup fails\\n\\n**django/conf/urls/i18n.py**: Internationalization\\n  - `i18n_patterns(*urls, prefix_default_language=True)`: Wraps patterns with language prefix support\\n  - Returns list of URLResolver with LocalePrefixPattern\\n  - `is_language_prefix_patterns_used(urlconf)`: Checks if i18n_patterns is active\\n\\n### Historical Context: patterns() Function\\n\\nThe deprecated `patterns()` function (Django < 1.10, mentioned in docs/releases/1.8.txt and docs/releases/1.9.txt) took a prefix argument to prepend to view paths. For example:\\n```python\\nurlpatterns = patterns('myapp.views',\\n    url('^$', 'myview'),\\n    url('^other/$', 'otherview'),\\n)\\n```\\nThis was replaced with explicit module paths in each pattern:\\n```python\\nurlpatterns = [\\n    path('', 'myapp.views.myview'),\\n    path('other/', 'myapp.views.otherview'),\\n]\\n```\\nThe current implementation completely eliminates this prefix concept in favor of direct view references or callables.\\n\\n### URL Resolution Chain\\n\\n1. **Configuration**: `urlpatterns` list contains URLPattern and URLResolver instances created via `path()`, `re_path()`, and `include()`\\n2. **Initial Resolution**: `resolve(path)` calls `get_resolver(ROOT_URLCONF).resolve(path)`\\n3. **Pattern Matching**: Root URLResolver iterates through url_patterns, calling `pattern.resolve()` on each\\n4. **Recursive Resolution**: For URLResolver patterns (from include()), continues recursively through nested url_patterns\\n5. **Match Processing**: RegexPattern/RoutePattern.match() extracts path args and kwargs\\n6. **Return**: ResolverMatch object with resolved view and parameters\\n7. **Reverse Lookup**: Cached `_reverse_dict` and `_namespace_dict` enable efficient URL reversal\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1307,"cache_read_input_tokens":87560,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1307},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a6f560ee-1bd0-4b5b-8a16-c84232586af3","uuid":"508351c9-ad40-4f29-a3b8-9498568d49c1"}

For example:\\n```python\\nurlpatterns = patterns('myapp.views',\\n    url('^$', 'myview'),\\n    url('^other/$', 'otherview'),\\n)\\n```\\nThis was replaced with explicit module paths in each pattern:\\n```python\\nurlpatterns = [\\n    path('', 'myapp.views.myview'),\\n    path('other/', 'myapp.views.otherview'),\\n]\\n```\\nThe current implementation completely eliminates this prefix concept in favor of direct view references or callables.\\n\\n### URL Resolution Chain\\n\\n1. **Configuration**: `urlpatterns` list contains URLPattern and URLResolver instances created via `path()`, `re_path()`, and `include()`\\n2. **Initial Resolution**: `resolve(path)` calls `get_resolver(ROOT_URLCONF).resolve(path)`\\n3. **Pattern Matching**: Root URLResolver iterates through url_patterns, calling `pattern.resolve()` on each\\n4. **Recursive Resolution**: For URLResolver patterns (from include()), continues recursively through nested url_patterns\\n5. **Match Processing**: RegexPattern/RoutePattern.match() extracts path args and kwargs\\n6. **Return**: ResolverMatch object with resolved view and parameters\\n7. **Reverse Lookup**: Cached `_reverse_dict` and `_namespace_dict` enable efficient URL reversal\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
